msg:[Naked Ridge] in Wuxiang Mountain
The air is fresh and quiet without crowds

The service is perfect. The shuttle bus is always on call. Entering the lobby is very ceremonial. I soak my hands in the water with newly picked peach blossoms to wash away the fatigue from the journey.

We arrived early and we were checked in in advance. The floor heating and air conditioning were turned on early in the room. As soon as we entered the room, we felt the warmth. The peach blossoms on both sides of the small courtyard happened to be in full bloom, just like in the book "Peach Blossom Spring"

There are many activities (the last picture is attached with an activity schedule), which is suitable for walking the baby. The baby can play in the amusement park, and I can do puzzles and take handicraft classes outside. You can free your hands even if you are raising a baby alone, which is touching

One-on-one butler Lcey provides 24-hour WeChat online service and gave a small gift and surprise when checking out.

The breakfast is also quite rich, and the waiter will also thoughtfully tell you that you can come back to eat at any time before 10:30. If the baby is not full, he can help you pack it away.

Naked Ridge is really suitable for walking kids. There are both outdoor and indoor children's parks. The cute pet parks are full of small animals. They can wander around freely. No matter which area you are in, there are staff who will come to ask if you need a connection. In the car, you can see mineral water and scented tea everywhere... When we were driving out of the park, we met the staff all the way. They all nodded and waved to our car enthusiastically, which made me feel embarrassed...

Maybe it's just luck that I came here this time. The cherry blossoms and peach blossoms are in full bloom. All the free activities in the handicraft workshop have just been implemented. In addition, there are very few people here on weekdays. You can really feel the slowed down time in the mountains in spring. , breathe and relax freely in the pure mountains and wilderness...

msg:It was a perfect holiday experience. Driving into Wuxiang Mountain Scenic Area was like entering a paradise, and Naked Ridge was like a fairy resort in a paradise lying quietly in this piece of mountains and waters. We chose to live in a mountain courtyard, with unique fences and wooden doors, private and comfortable courtyard space, and a warm and spacious 60-square-meter room, which made us quite satisfied. The breakfast was great, and it was very pure and exquisite. I liked the American breakfast and Chinese beef noodles very much. It was hard to imagine that the hotel could grasp the taste of different styles of breakfast in China and the West so well. The activities in the hotel were very rich: cycling, hiking, plant rubbings, archery, feeding small animals, grooming ponies, red wine tasting, roasting marshmallows... I was also very lucky to win the first place in the archery competition and won a small doll gift. The children were very happy! From morning to night, both adults and children had a lot of fun. At night, I returned to the room, soaked comfortably in the round bathtub for a while, and then put on pajamas to fall asleep. The holiday life was so wonderful and fulfilling!
If there are places that can be done better, first, the hotel is in a natural environment, we can see a lot of insects outdoors, and we saw a lot of big bees and bumblebees several times, which made us feel a little scared; second, there is no garbage bag in the trash can in the room. I can feel that it is for the concept of environmental protection, but when eating the welcome fruit, I really can't bear to throw the peel directly into such a beautiful trash can. Fortunately, I prepared a garbage bag.
Finally, I would like to thank every staff member here, especially our exclusive housekeeper Miss Elsa on this vacation. She has the same English name as my daughter, and we are very lucky. Thank you for her careful answers and meticulous service. Thank you also to the manager Mr. Patrick, his gentleman service and interaction with the children are really great! There are also service staff who help us clean the room, and staff who carefully disinfect the bathtub. At the same time, I would like to thank the staff of the Western restaurant and the driver of the battery car in the hotel for their meticulous and patient service!
I believe that I will choose Naked Ridge again and come to this place full of beauty, relaxation and happiness again. I can't wait to look forward to the next trip to Naked Ridge!

msg:In the hot summer, I lived in Naked Ridge with my baby and 80+ parents for two days. The overall feeling is very good, and the elderly have a good time. A few things stand out:
1. The resort is located in a large area in Wuxiang Mountain. Various houses are integrated with the landscape and terrain, which is very natural and also has a sense of design. We booked the mountain courtyard and the forest hut at the same time, and we prefer the mountain courtyard
2. Although it is the peak summer tourist season, there are fewer guests than expected, and the whole resort is very clean. Whether it is a golf course, lawn or a pet park, you can enjoy a private corner wherever you go
3. The green ecology in the village is very good, there are small scenes everywhere, the small animals are clean, and the alpacas are free to graze outside during the day. Accompanied by the sound of cicadas, it is the beautiful appearance of summer
4. The butler team Molly/Ricky is very friendly and responds in a timely manner, leaving a good impression on my parents. The buffet breakfast is small and beautiful, with a complete variety and good taste. Chinese food is also good, but the price is more expensive
5. It is very close to Wuxiang Temple, about 900 meters away from the residential area. But in the past, I found out that Wuxiang Temple had been temporarily closed in July, leaving a little regret.
